Livability ~51% (family, location, condition, outdoor) · Financial / resale ~49% (price vs local €/m², value judgment, energy, running costs, tenure, legal). Tuned for a live-in home for one adult + a 3-yo, sold in 5–10 years. Price vs local €/m², family, location, energy (incl. upgrade-potential bonus), tenure, running costs and outdoor are computed from the data; value (a condition-adjusted judgment), condition and legal are scored by hand.
Conf. = data-verification confidence: how many of 6 key fields (price, area, WOZ, energy label, ground/tenure, beds) are verified against an independent source. ✓N/6, green ≥5 · amber ≥3 · red <3; ⚠ = a source conflict. Hover for which fields are unverified.

NEW from Funda digest 16-06. 1083 BP Amsterdam (Buitenveldert-Oost). 83 m2, 4 kamers (3 slaapkamers = 3 bed), bouwjaar 1959 portiekflat, VOLLEDIG GERENOVEERD in 2019 + extra kamer 2023 met HR++ beglazing (move-in ready). Asking EUR 525k k.k. (te koop sinds 15-06, Burgemeester Vastgoed) = EUR 6,325/m2. VALUE: asking is ~12% BELOW WOZ EUR 600k (peildatum 01-01-2025, huispedia/LV-WOZ) and below Huispedia woningwaarde EUR 544k-632k. FLAG: classic invite-overbid pricing — 89% of homes in this buurt sell ABOVE asking and Huispedia models a winning bid ~EUR 590k; budget vs ~EUR 590k+, NOT the EUR 525k vraagprijs. CONFLICT: a stale aggregator snippet showed WOZ EUR 482k (likely an older peildatum); the property page states EUR 600k @ 01-01-2025 — reconcile on wozwaardeloket.nl before any offer. RISK (top): ERFPACHT — canon is AFGEKOCHT only until 30-11-2058 under Algemene Bepalingen 2000 (voortdurend), NOT eeuwigdurend afgekocht; after 2058 a new canon/buy-off applies — a finite ~32-yr horizon that can affect future financing/resale; verify regime on the akte/Amsterdam erfpacht map. VvE healthy: professionally managed (Pro VvE Beheer), 48 woningen, servicekosten EUR 170.58/mo (verified). Note: within a Schiphol aircraft-noise zone. Energy label C with some upside to B/A (partly addressed in the 2019 reno). Bike: ~6 min to Zuidas (station Zuid 1.96km), ~13 min to Emmakade 33 (est). Best-condition and joint-largest of today's batch.

Energy label E (geregistreerd, EP-Online via drimble) — weak; a 1966 portiek/galerijflat can in principle be improved (HR++ glazing/insulation) but that is VvE-driven, so easy-upgrade upside is LIMITED for a single owner. RISK: ground = Amstelveen, so almost certainly EIGEN GROND (no Amsterdam erfpacht) — a clear legal plus, but confirm on the akte. VvE EUR/mo unknown (est EUR 175). Condition: 1966 + label E suggests largely original/dated — budget for modernisation (keuken/badkamer/beglazing). Bike: ~10 min to Emmakade 33, ~11 min to Zuidas (est from postcode). 3 bedrooms comfortably meets the original 2-bed+ brief.

VERIFIED via official Funda (id 44469451, Beschikbaar, on Funda since 22 May): HOEKmaisonnette, 85 m² (not 93), 2 bed (3 kamers), label A (roof/wall/double-glazing insulation), 1951, eigen grond, VvE only €78/mo (healthy — reserve fund + maintenance plan). €5,706/m² — below Randwijck-Oost avg €6,613. Beschermd stadsgezicht — interior free, street-facing exterior needs permits (see heritage_beschermd_stadsgezicht.md); verify existing kunststof kozijnen were permitted. Stadshart & Zuidas by bike. Top pick. VIEWING 2026-06-02 (Max): interior dated, needs FULL gut renovation — budget €110k–€140k incl. new kitchen/bath/electrics/plumbing/floors (1951 build → asbestos survey + full rewire likely; +15-20% contingency). Interior gut needs no permit (heritage = street-facing only). True all-in ~€7,000/m² (>Randwijck-Oost avg €6,613) — below-market thesis only holds if reno is negotiated off asking. RODENT FLAG: steel wool stuffing corner holes (seller managing a recurring problem) + waste container directly in front = active mouse/rat source. Gut is ideal moment to rodent-proof unit (steel wool+mortar, mesh over penetrations), but source needs VvE/gemeente collective fix (container) — sealing own unit won't fully solve. TODO before advancing: VvE notulen (check ongedierte history), bouwkundige keuring + pest inspection, force seller disclosure, re-price offer well below €485k. VALUATION (2026-06-02): asking €485k = €5,706/m², ~14% under Randwijck-Oost renovated avg €6,613/m² — but that avg is move-in stock. Pricing the €110-140k gut: renovated ref ~€562k (85m²×€6,613) − ~€125k reno = ~€437k pay-market CEILING; fixer €/m² comps €4,600-5,000 → €391-425k; WOZ €446k (ask +8.7%). FAIR AS-IS ≈ €390-420k. STRATEGY: open €400k, target settle €420-435k, walk-away €440k (above that you pay renovated-market price for a gut job). Conditional on NEN2580 area (85 vs 98m²), asbestinventarisatie, VvE jaarrekening+MJOP+notulen (rodent history), kunststof-kozijnen permit. Docs requested from verkoopmakelaar 2026-06-02. DOCS REVIEWED 2026-06-02 (seller set: vragenlijst, VvE notulen 2026, balans 2025, MJOP 2020-30, energielabel, akte, plattegrond): EIGEN GROND confirmed (akte; only a benign 1950 Province-NH electricity easement). Usable area = 82.1 m² GO per energielabel (the 98 m² was gross/BAG — resolved). Label A registered 23-08-2023, valid to 24-11-2032, but gas + 0% renewable, 150.5 kWh/m². RISKS: (1) PEST DISCLOSURE CONFLICT — vragenlijst says 'geen overlast ongedierte', contradicts steel-wool + container seen on viewing → get in writing. (2) Disclosed LEAK bathroom→kitchen. (3) Disclosed (verborgen) scheuren/beschadigingen in unit. (4) VvE reserve dangerously low (~€1k end-2025; was negative 2024 after €34k garage-street repaving funded by member loans; statutory norm €11,777/yr vs ~€3,400 added); roof-ridge (nok) replacement agreed but unfunded → suppletie likely; this unit = 21/170 (~12%) share. (7) Floor-plan file named 'Oostzijde 92 A' (different address) — confirm it depicts CvC40. Still missing: splitsingsakte+tekening, NEN2580, WOZ-beschikking, insurance polis. VERDICT: conditionally worth it at ~€390-405k with bouwkundige keuring + asbest + splitsingsakte + VvE roof/suppletie + written pest clarification as conditions. Methodology (model v4): Weighted score out of 10, tuned for a live-in home for one adult + a 3-yo (shared custody), sold in 5–10 years. Two clusters — livability ~51%: Family fit & space (17%), Location & commute (15%), Condition (13%), Outdoor space (6%); financial / resale ~49%: Price vs local €/m² (9%), Value judgment (10%), Energy label (10%), Running costs (8%), Tenure / erfpacht (7%), Legal / title risk (5%). v4 change: €/m² now outweighs the raw WOZ premium — Price vs local €/m² is the asking-vs-WOZ premium centred on the property's city median, so WOZ serves only as the location/size-aware normaliser, not a stale absolute anchor. Running costs are the full owner monthly = VvE + heating advance + WOZ-driven owner taxes (OZB ≈0.063% Amstelveen / ≈0.058% Amsterdam + eigenwoningforfait 0.35% × ~37% box-1), so a higher WOZ raises carrying cost. Price vs €/m², family, location, energy, tenure, running costs and outdoor are computed from the underlying data; value (a condition-adjusted judgment overlay: over-priced-for-condition, bidding-war temper), condition and legal are scored by hand against the rubric. Blank criteria renormalise over the ones that are scored. WOZ values are the official 2025 Kadaster LV-WOZ assessments; OZB/forfait are 2025 rates (tunable) — re-check at offer time. All data as of 2026-07-05.
